# Shopify Product Proof / Measurement Readiness Audit

Created: 2026-05-24T14:20:03.695Z

Scope: read-only Shopify Admin API scan of ACTIVE products using API version `2025-10`.

Limits: product pagination fetched all returned ACTIVE products. Per product, the script requested up to 100 images and 250 metafields. 1 product(s) hit a per-product pagination limit and may need a deeper follow-up.

Signals audited:

- Measurement-related product metafields: namespace, key, type, or value matching measurement/ruler/size/inches/cm/height/width/length/dimensions terms.
- Product image alt text or filename matching measurement/ruler/size/inches/cm/height/width/length/dimensions terms.
- Product description copy that references buyer-facing photos/images/measurements/sizes/dimensions, or includes explicit dimension values.

| Metric | Count |
| --- | ---: |
| Active products audited | 1784 |
| Products with measurement-related metafields | 1587 |
| Products with measurement/ruler/size image alt text or filename signals | 117 |

| Products missing all audited signals | 171 |
| Products where image/metafield pagination limit was reached | 1 |
